{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01TBehUk8LqdTLmTviFgmipm","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01Y6PoGW9uvRkhTJ3yyY91uX","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/documentation.md","content":"# Envoy External Processing (ext_proc) Filter Migration Guide\n## Version 1.30.0 → 1.31.0\n\n## Overview\n\nThis guide documents the changes to the Envoy External Processing HTTP filter between v1.30.0 (April 2024) and v1.31.0 (July 2024). The ext_proc filter enables external gRPC services to process HTTP requests and responses in flexible ways.\n\n**Summary of Major Changes:**\n- New `observability_mode` feature for monitoring HTTP traffic without blocking\n- Enhanced route cache control via new `route_cache_action` enum field\n- Support for deferred stream closure in observability mode\n- HTTP status code improvement for timeout errors\n- Deprecated `async_mode` in favor of `observability_mode`\n\n---\n\n## Breaking Changes\n\n### 1. HTTP Status Code for External Processor Timeouts\n\n**Impact:** Applications expecting `500 Internal Server Error` for ext_proc timeouts will now receive `504 Gateway Timeout`.\n\n**Details:**\n- **v1.30.0:** Timeout errors in external processor returned `500 Internal Server Error`\n- **v1.31.0:** Timeout errors now return `504 Gateway Timeout`\n- This is semantically more correct as it indicates the upstream service (external processor) is not responding\n\n**Migration Action:**\n- Update monitoring/alerting rules that depend on HTTP status codes for ext_proc failures\n- Adjust client-side retry logic if it differentiates between 5xx error codes\n- No configuration changes required\n\n**Source Files:**\n- `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.cc` - Filter implementation\n\n---\n\n## Deprecated Features\n\n### 1. `disable_clear_route_cache` Field (Field 11)\n\n**Status:** Deprecated but still functional with migration support\n\n**Details:**\n- **v1.30.0:** Boolean field that prevents route cache from being cleared\n- **v1.31.0:** Marked for deprecation via UDPA field migration annotation\n- **Recommended Replacement:** Use `route_cache_action` field instead\n\n**Migration Path:**\n```protobuf\n// v1.30.0 style (deprecated in v1.31.0)\ndisable_clear_route_cache: true\n\n// v1.31.0 style (recommended)\nroute_cache_action: RETAIN\n```\n\n**Behavior Mapping:**\n- `disable_clear_route_cache: true` → `route_cache_action: RETAIN`\n- `disable_clear_route_cache: false` (or unset) → `route_cache_action: DEFAULT`\n\n**Migration Timeline:**\n- v1.31.0: Both fields accepted, migration annotation present\n- Future versions: `disable_clear_route_cache` may be removed\n\n**YAML Configuration Example:**\n\nBefore:\n```yaml\nname: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\ntyped_config:\n  \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: ext_proc_service\n  disable_clear_route_cache: true\n```\n\nAfter:\n```yaml\nname: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\ntyped_config:\n  \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: ext_proc_service\n  route_cache_action: RETAIN\n```\n\n**Source Files:**\n- `api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/ext_proc.proto` (lines 250-251)\n- `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.cc` - Initialization logic\n- `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.h` - Field declaration\n\n### 2. `async_mode` (Field 4, marked as reserved in ExtProcOverrides)\n\n**Status:** Not implemented, marked as hidden\n\n**Details:**\n- Remains marked as `[#not-implemented-hide:]` in the ExtProcOverrides message\n- The new `observability_mode` at the filter configuration level provides similar functionality\n- Note: `async_mode` was never actually implemented in the filter\n\n**Migration Action:**\n- If you attempted to use `async_mode` in ExtProcOverrides, it will continue to be ignored\n- To enable asynchronous-like behavior, use `observability_mode` at the filter config level (see New Features section below)\n\n---\n\n## New Features\n\n### 1. Observability Mode\n\n**Availability:** New in v1.31.0\n\n**Purpose:** Enables \"Send and Go\" mode for external processors that only observe/monitor traffic without modifying it.\n\n**Configuration Field:**\n```protobuf\n// Field 17 in ExternalProcessor message\nbool observability_mode = 17;\n```\n\n**Key Characteristics:**\n- External processor receives HTTP request and response data without sending back responses\n- Messages are sent without pausing on filter chain iteration\n- Only `STREAMED` body processing mode is supported (other body modes are ignored)\n- `NONE` body mode (skip body) continues to work as expected\n- External processor may still close the stream to signal completion\n- Flow control is being developed but not yet complete\n\n**YAML Configuration Example:**\n```yaml\nname: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\ntyped_config:\n  \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: ext_proc_observability_service\n  processing_mode:\n    request_header_mode: SEND\n    response_header_mode: SEND\n    request_body_mode: STREAMED\n    response_body_mode: STREAMED\n  observability_mode: true\n  deferred_close_timeout:\n    seconds: 5\n```\n\n**Supported Processing Modes with observability_mode:**\n| Mode | Result | Notes |\n|------|--------|-------|\n| request_header_mode: SEND | ✓ Sent | Headers always sent |\n| response_header_mode: SEND | ✓ Sent | Headers always sent |\n| request_body_mode: STREAMED | ✓ Sent | Body streamed without blocking |\n| request_body_mode: BUFFERED | ⚠️ Ignored | Falls back to streaming behavior |\n| request_body_mode: BUFFERED_PARTIAL | ⚠️ Ignored | Falls back to streaming behavior |\n| request_body_mode: NONE | ✓ Skipped | Body not sent |\n| request_trailer_mode: SEND | ✓ Sent | Trailers sent if present |\n\n**Message Format:**\n- Requests include `observability_mode: true` flag in the ProcessingRequest\n- ProcessingResponse is ignored/not expected from the processor\n- Timeouts (message_timeout) do not apply in observability mode\n\n**Practical Use Cases:**\n- Monitoring/logging services that observe request/response headers and bodies\n- Distributed tracing integration\n- Audit logging systems\n- Traffic analytics services\n- Network diagnostic tools\n\n**Implementation Details:**\n- Uses `DeferredDeletableStream` wrapper for managing stream lifecycle\n- `ThreadLocalStreamManager` handles deferred stream closure\n- Streams may be held open longer than regular client-to-backend streams\n- `deferred_close_timeout` controls maximum stream lifetime\n\n**Source Files:**\n- `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.h` (lines 212, 275)\n- `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.cc` - observability mode handling\n\n### 2. Route Cache Action Enum\n\n**Availability:** New in v1.31.0\n\n**Purpose:** Provides explicit control over when the route cache should be cleared based on external processor responses.\n\n**Configuration Field:**\n```protobuf\n// Field 18 in ExternalProcessor message\nenum RouteCacheAction {\n  // The default behavior (consistent with v1.30.0)\n  DEFAULT = 0;\n\n  // Always clear the route cache\n  CLEAR = 1;\n\n  // Never clear the route cache (replaces disable_clear_route_cache)\n  RETAIN = 2;\n}\n\nRouteCacheAction route_cache_action = 18;\n```\n\n**Behavior Details:**\n\n#### DEFAULT Mode (Recommended for most users)\n- Route cache is cleared **only if** the external processor sets `clear_route_cache: true` in the response\n- Maintains backward compatibility with v1.30.0 behavior\n- Most flexible approach allowing per-request control\n\n```yaml\nroute_cache_action: DEFAULT\n```\n\n#### CLEAR Mode\n- Route cache is **always cleared** when external processor responds to request headers\n- Ignores the `clear_route_cache` field in processor response\n- Use when header modifications always require route recomputation\n\n```yaml\nroute_cache_action: CLEAR\n```\n\n#### RETAIN Mode\n- Route cache is **never cleared** regardless of processor response\n- Ignores the `clear_route_cache` field in processor response\n- Use when you know header modifications won't affect routing\n\n```yaml\nroute_cache_action: RETAIN\n```\n\n**When Route Cache Matters:**\nThe route cache affects whether modified headers trigger route recomputation:\n- Headers like `:authority`, `:scheme`, `:method`, and user-defined routing headers may affect route selection\n- Route modifications from external processor may be ignored if cache is not cleared\n- Example: If external processor changes `:authority` header, route cache must be cleared for new route to take effect\n\n**Interaction with Upstream Filters:**\n- Route cache clearing is ignored when ext_proc filter is in upstream filter chain\n- Statistics are tracked: `clear_route_cache_upstream_ignored`\n\n**YAML Configuration Examples:**\n\n```yaml\n# Example 1: Default behavior (recommended)\nname: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\ntyped_config:\n  \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: ext_proc_service\n  route_cache_action: DEFAULT\n\n# Example 2: Always clear route cache\nname: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\ntyped_config:\n  \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: ext_proc_service\n  route_cache_action: CLEAR\n\n# Example 3: Never clear route cache\nname: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\ntyped_config:\n  \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: ext_proc_service\n  route_cache_action: RETAIN\n```\n\n**Constraints:**\n- `disable_clear_route_cache` and `route_cache_action` are mutually exclusive\n- Attempting to set both will result in an error: \"disable_clear_route_cache and route_cache_action can not be set at the same time\"\n- If `disable_clear_route_cache: true` is set, it is automatically converted to `route_cache_action: RETAIN`\n\n**Source Files:**\n- `api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/ext_proc.proto` (lines 105-120, 253-258)\n- `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.cc` - Route cache action handling\n- `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/processor_state.cc` - Route cache clearing logic\n\n### 3. Deferred Close Timeout\n\n**Availability:** New in v1.31.0\n\n**Purpose:** Controls the maximum duration a gRPC stream to the external processor may remain open in observability mode.\n\n**Configuration Field:**\n```protobuf\n// Field 19 in ExternalProcessor message\ngoogle.protobuf.Duration deferred_close_timeout = 19;\n```\n\n**Default Value:**\n- `5000` milliseconds (5 seconds) if not specified\n\n**Why It's Needed:**\nIn observability mode, streams may be held open longer than the client-to-backend stream lifetime. This timeout prevents indefinite stream lifetime.\n\n**When It Applies:**\n- Only used in `observability_mode: true` configurations\n- Ignored in standard synchronous mode\n\n**YAML Configuration Example:**\n```yaml\nname: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\ntyped_config:\n  \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: ext_proc_service\n  observability_mode: true\n  deferred_close_timeout:\n    seconds: 10\n    # Optional: nanos: 0\n\n# Alternative: 2.5 seconds\ndeferred_close_timeout:\n  seconds: 2\n  nanos: 500000000\n\n# Alternative: 100 milliseconds\ndeferred_close_timeout:\n  nanos: 100000000\n```\n\n**Validation Rules:**\n- Maximum allowed: 3600 seconds (1 hour)\n- Minimum allowed: 0 (immediate timeout, useful for testing)\n- Values follow protobuf Duration format validation\n\n**Implementation Details:**\n- Uses `DeferredDeletableStream` struct to wrap streams with timeout\n- `ThreadLocalStreamManager` manages deferred closure with timers\n- Timer name: `derferred_close_timer` (note: contains typo in source code)\n\n**Source Files:**\n- `api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/ext_proc.proto` (lines 260-265)\n- `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.h` (lines 150-171, 214, 278)\n- `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.cc` - Deferred close handling\n\n---\n\n## Migration Steps\n\n### Step 1: Audit Current Configuration (v1.30.0)\n\nIdentify all ext_proc filter configurations in your Envoy setup:\n\n```bash\n# Find all ext_proc filter configurations\ngrep -r \"envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\" /path/to/configs/\ngrep -r \"ext_proc\" /path/to/configs/\n```\n\nDocument:\n- All `disable_clear_route_cache` settings\n- All `async_mode` references (should be none if not implemented)\n- Whether `observability_mode`-like behavior is needed\n\n### Step 2: Plan Field Migrations\n\n#### For `disable_clear_route_cache` Users:\n\n**Option A: Migrate to `route_cache_action`** (Recommended)\n```yaml\n# Old (v1.30.0)\ndisable_clear_route_cache: false\n\n# New (v1.31.0)\nroute_cache_action: DEFAULT\n```\n\n```yaml\n# Old (v1.30.0)\ndisable_clear_route_cache: true\n\n# New (v1.31.0)\nroute_cache_action: RETAIN\n```\n\n**Option B: No Action Required**\n- Both fields will be supported in v1.31.0\n- Migration can be deferred to a future version\n- Automatic conversion happens: `disable_clear_route_cache: true` → `route_cache_action: RETAIN`\n\n#### For `async_mode` Users:\n- If used in ExtProcOverrides, the field will continue to be ignored\n- No migration path exists yet (async_mode was never implemented)\n- For monitoring use cases, consider `observability_mode` instead\n\n### Step 3: Enable New Features (Optional)\n\nIf you need observability/monitoring capabilities:\n\n```yaml\nname: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\ntyped_config:\n  \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: ext_proc_monitoring_service\n  processing_mode:\n    request_header_mode: SEND\n    response_header_mode: SEND\n    request_body_mode: STREAMED\n    response_body_mode: STREAMED\n  observability_mode: true\n  deferred_close_timeout:\n    seconds: 5\n```\n\n### Step 4: Update External Processor Service\n\n**If Using Standard Synchronous Mode:**\n- No changes required to external processor service\n- Continue implementing `ProcessingRequest` → `ProcessingResponse` handlers\n\n**If Using Observability Mode:**\n- Update external processor to handle `observability_mode: true` flag in requests\n- Process and log/monitor data from requests\n- Do NOT send back `ProcessingResponse` messages (they will be ignored)\n- May close stream early with `grpc.stream.close()`\n\n### Step 5: Test Configuration\n\n**Validation Steps:**\n1. Validate configuration syntax (proto validation)\n2. Test with new Envoy v1.31.0 binary\n3. Verify external processor connectivity and behavior\n4. Test header modifications with new route cache action setting\n5. Monitor HTTP status codes for timeout errors (now 504 instead of 500)\n\n**Test Case Examples:**\n\n```yaml\n# Test 1: Route cache action behavior\n---\nname: Test DEFAULT route cache action\nhttp_filters:\n  - name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n    typed_config:\n      \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n      grpc_service:\n        envoy_grpc:\n          cluster_name: ext_proc\n      route_cache_action: DEFAULT\n      processing_mode:\n        request_header_mode: SEND\n\n# External processor modifies :authority header\n# Route cache should clear ONLY if response has clear_route_cache: true\n\n---\nname: Test CLEAR route cache action\nhttp_filters:\n  - name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n    typed_config:\n      \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n      grpc_service:\n        envoy_grpc:\n          cluster_name: ext_proc\n      route_cache_action: CLEAR\n      processing_mode:\n        request_header_mode: SEND\n\n# External processor modifies :authority header\n# Route cache should ALWAYS clear, regardless of response\n\n---\nname: Test RETAIN route cache action\nhttp_filters:\n  - name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n    typed_config:\n      \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n      grpc_service:\n        envoy_grpc:\n          cluster_name: ext_proc\n      route_cache_action: RETAIN\n      processing_mode:\n        request_header_mode: SEND\n\n# External processor modifies headers\n# Route cache should NEVER clear\n\n---\nname: Test observability mode\nhttp_filters:\n  - name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n    typed_config:\n      \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n      grpc_service:\n        envoy_grpc:\n          cluster_name: ext_proc_monitoring\n      processing_mode:\n        request_body_mode: STREAMED\n        response_body_mode: STREAMED\n      observability_mode: true\n\n# Processor receives requests but doesn't send responses\n# Verify: stream closure after deferred_close_timeout\n```\n\n### Step 6: Monitor and Validate\n\n**Metrics to Monitor:**\n\n```\n# Route cache action metrics (new in v1.31.0)\nenvoy_http_ext_proc_clear_route_cache_ignored{...}\nenvoy_http_ext_proc_clear_route_cache_disabled{...}\nenvoy_http_ext_proc_clear_route_cache_upstream_ignored{...}\n\n# Existing metrics still available\nenvoy_http_ext_proc_streams_started{...}\nenvoy_http_ext_proc_stream_msgs_sent{...}\nenvoy_http_ext_proc_stream_msgs_received{...}\nenvoy_http_ext_proc_streams_failed{...}\nenvoy_http_ext_proc_message_timeouts{...}\n\n# Status code changes\nenvoy_http_<stat_prefix>_response_code_504{...}  # New in v1.31.0 (previously 500)\n```\n\n---\n\n## Behavioral Changes Summary\n\n### Status Code Changes\n\n| Scenario | v1.30.0 | v1.31.0 | Impact |\n|----------|---------|---------|--------|\n| External processor timeout | 500 | 504 | Upstream service unavailable |\n| gRPC stream error | 500 | 500 | Stream connection failure |\n| Failure mode allow | Pass-through | Pass-through | No change |\n\n**Implications:**\n- Client-side retry logic may need updates\n- Load balancer health checks may treat 504 differently\n- Monitoring/alerting rules should be reviewed\n\n### gRPC Tracing Context Headers\n\n**v1.31.0 Enhancement:**\n- `AsyncStreamImpl` and `GoogleAsyncStreamImpl` now propagate tracing context headers in bidirectional streams\n- Applies when using Envoy gRPC client or Google C++ gRPC client\n- Previously, tracing context was not being set for external services like ext_proc\n- This improves distributed tracing across ext_proc services\n\n---\n\n## Configuration Field Reference\n\n### Complete v1.31.0 ExternalProcessor Message\n\n```protobuf\nmessage ExternalProcessor {\n  // [1] Required: gRPC service configuration\n  config.core.v3.GrpcService grpc_service = 1;\n\n  // [2] Default: false - Allow processing to continue on gRPC errors\n  bool failure_mode_allow = 2;\n\n  // [3] Default: SEND for headers, NONE for bodies - Processing modes\n  ProcessingMode processing_mode = 3;\n\n  // [5] Default: [] - Request attributes to send to processor\n  repeated string request_attributes = 5;\n\n  // [6] Default: [] - Response attributes to send to processor\n  repeated string response_attributes = 6;\n\n  // [7] Default: 200ms - Timeout for processor messages\n  google.protobuf.Duration message_timeout = 7;\n\n  // [8] Default: \"\" - Additional stats prefix\n  string stat_prefix = 8;\n\n  // [9] Default: allow all except protected headers - Header mutation rules\n  config.common.mutation_rules.v3.HeaderMutationRules mutation_rules = 9;\n\n  // [10] Default: 0 (disabled) - Max override message timeout\n  google.protobuf.Duration max_message_timeout = 10;\n\n  // [11] DEPRECATED: Use route_cache_action instead\n  // Default: false - Don't clear route cache when processor requests\n  bool disable_clear_route_cache = 11;\n\n  // [12] Default: forward all - Header forwarding rules\n  HeaderForwardingRules forward_rules = 12;\n\n  // [13] Default: {} - Additional metadata for logging\n  google.protobuf.Struct filter_metadata = 13;\n\n  // [14] Default: false - Allow processor to override processing mode\n  bool allow_mode_override = 14;\n\n  // [15] Default: false - Ignore immediate_response from processor\n  bool disable_immediate_response = 15;\n\n  // [16] Default: [] - Dynamic metadata options\n  MetadataOptions metadata_options = 16;\n\n  // [17] Default: false - NEW: Observability/monitoring mode (Send and Go)\n  bool observability_mode = 17;\n\n  // [18] NEW: Route cache action (replaces disable_clear_route_cache)\n  // Default: DEFAULT\n  RouteCacheAction route_cache_action = 18;\n\n  // [19] NEW: Stream deferred close timeout in observability mode\n  // Default: 5000ms\n  google.protobuf.Duration deferred_close_timeout = 19;\n}\n\nenum RouteCacheAction {\n  DEFAULT = 0;  // Clear only if processor requests\n  CLEAR = 1;    // Always clear\n  RETAIN = 2;   // Never clear\n}\n\nmessage HeaderForwardingRules {\n  type.matcher.v3.ListStringMatcher allowed_headers = 1;\n  type.matcher.v3.ListStringMatcher disallowed_headers = 2;\n}\n\nmessage MetadataOptions {\n  message MetadataNamespaces {\n    repeated string untyped = 1;\n    repeated string typed = 2;\n  }\n  MetadataNamespaces forwarding_namespaces = 1;\n  MetadataNamespaces receiving_namespaces = 2;\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Testing Recommendations\n\n### Unit Test Strategy\n\n1. **Route Cache Action Tests**\n   - Verify DEFAULT mode respects `clear_route_cache` in response\n   - Verify CLEAR mode always clears regardless of response\n   - Verify RETAIN mode never clears regardless of response\n   - Test with upstream filter chain (should ignore all modes)\n\n2. **Observability Mode Tests**\n   - Verify `observability_mode: true` sends messages without waiting for responses\n   - Verify only STREAMED body mode is actually used\n   - Verify BUFFERED/BUFFERED_PARTIAL fall back to streaming\n   - Verify NONE mode skips body processing\n   - Verify stream closure after `deferred_close_timeout`\n\n3. **Status Code Tests**\n   - Verify timeout errors return 504 instead of 500\n   - Verify other errors still return appropriate codes\n   - Verify failure_mode_allow still works\n\n4. **Backward Compatibility Tests**\n   - Verify old configs with `disable_clear_route_cache` still work\n   - Verify automatic conversion to RETAIN works\n   - Verify both fields can't be set simultaneously\n\n### Integration Test Strategy\n\n1. **External Processor Integration**\n   - Test with real external processor service\n   - Verify request/response format unchanged\n   - Verify header modifications work as before\n   - Test with observability_mode processor\n\n2. **Header Modification Tests**\n   - Modify :authority header and verify route recalculation\n   - Modify custom routing headers\n   - Verify route cache clearing behavior with each action mode\n\n3. **Performance Tests**\n   - Measure impact of observability_mode on throughput\n   - Compare stream closure behavior with deferred_close_timeout\n\n4. **Upgrade Tests**\n   - Run existing v1.30.0 configs on v1.31.0 binary\n   - Verify graceful behavior with new fields unset\n   - Test both field migration approaches\n\n---\n\n## Rollback Guidance\n\n### If Issues Occur\n\n**Option 1: Immediate Rollback**\n1. Revert to Envoy v1.30.0 binary\n2. No configuration changes needed (v1.30.0 ignores v1.31.0-only fields)\n3. Verify service stabilization\n\n**Option 2: Downgrade with Configuration Update**\nIf you updated configs to use v1.31.0 features:\n\n```yaml\n# Before rollback (v1.31.0 config)\nroute_cache_action: CLEAR\nobservability_mode: true\n\n# Rollback (v1.30.0 compatible)\ndisable_clear_route_cache: false  # Equivalent to DEFAULT\n# Remove observability_mode (not supported)\n# Remove deferred_close_timeout (not supported)\n```\n\n### Common Issues and Resolution\n\n**Issue: \"disable_clear_route_cache and route_cache_action can not be set at the same time\"**\n- **Cause:** Both fields set in configuration\n- **Fix:** Use only `route_cache_action`, remove `disable_clear_route_cache`\n- **Workaround:** Temporarily revert to v1.30.0\n\n**Issue: Observability mode processor not receiving messages**\n- **Cause:** Messages might be sent before stream is fully established\n- **Fix:** Add delay in processor startup or ensure it's listening before Envoy sends\n- **Fix:** Check that `processing_mode` is configured correctly\n\n**Issue: Stream timeouts in observability mode**\n- **Cause:** `deferred_close_timeout` too short for processor\n- **Fix:** Increase `deferred_close_timeout` value\n- **Example:** Increase from default 5s to 10s or more\n\n**Issue: Route cache not clearing as expected**\n- **Cause:** Wrong `route_cache_action` mode selected\n- **Debug:** Enable debug logging: `--log-level debug`\n- **Debug:** Check statistics: `clear_route_cache_ignored`, `clear_route_cache_disabled`\n\n---\n\n## Proto File Changes\n\n### Files Modified in v1.31.0\n\n#### `api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/ext_proc.proto`\n\n**Key Changes:**\n- Added import: `udpa/annotations/migrate.proto`\n- Updated `[#next-free-field]` comment: 18 → 20\n- `processing_mode.proto`\n\nThe ProcessingMode message remains unchanged in v1.31.0.\n\n---\n\n## Compatibility Matrix\n\n| Feature | v1.30.0 | v1.31.0 | Migration |\n|---------|---------|---------|-----------|\n| disable_clear_route_cache | ✓ | ✓ Deprecated | → route_cache_action: RETAIN |\n| route_cache_action | ✗ | ✓ New | Optional adoption |\n| observability_mode | ✗ | ✓ New | Opt-in feature |\n| deferred_close_timeout | ✗ | ✓ New | Only for observability_mode |\n| 500 timeout errors | ✓ | ✗ Changed to 504 | Monitoring/alerting updates |\n| Header mutation | ✓ | ✓ Unchanged | No action needed |\n| Streaming bodies | ✓ | ✓ Unchanged | No action needed |\n| Dynamic metadata | ✓ | ✓ Unchanged | No action needed |\n\n---\n\n## Best Practices for v1.31.0\n\n### 1. **Route Cache Management**\n- Use `route_cache_action: DEFAULT` for most cases (allows per-request control)\n- Use `route_cache_action: CLEAR` only if all processor responses require route recalculation\n- Use `route_cache_action: RETAIN` only if processor never modifies routing-relevant headers\n\n### 2. **Observability Mode**\n- Only enable for monitoring/logging processors\n- Don't enable if processor needs to modify requests/responses\n- Ensure processor implementation handles one-way messaging\n- Set appropriate `deferred_close_timeout` for your use case (5-10 seconds typical)\n\n### 3. **Processing Mode with Observability**\n- Limit to essential fields (headers, bodies needed for logging)\n- Avoid `BUFFERED` modes as they're converted to `STREAMED` anyway\n- Consider bandwidth impact of streaming large bodies\n\n### 4. **Monitoring and Alerting**\n- Update status code alerts (504 for timeouts, not 500)\n- Add metrics tracking for route cache actions\n- Monitor `deferred_close_timeout` for observability streams\n\n### 5. **Documentation**\n- Document which route cache action mode each processor requires\n- Maintain runbooks for migration issues\n- Track external processor compatibility with v1.31.0\n\n---\n\n## Additional Resources\n\n### Envoy Documentation\n- [ext_proc Filter Configuration Filter header with field definitions\n  - `ext_proc.cc` - Filter implementation logic\n  - `processor_state.cc` - Request/response processing and route cache handling\n\n### Release Notes\n- Envoy {"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01Y6PoGW9uvRkhTJ3yyY91uX","type":"tool_result","content":"File created successfully at: /workspace/documentation.md"}]},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"dd2176e2-e1b9-49fe-8e1d-3f775af76e9b","uuid":"5b08b1db-5d22-4c72-9881-8649d0894f19","tool_use_result":{"type":"create","filePath":"/workspace/documentation.md","content":"# Envoy External Processing (ext_proc) Filter Migration Guide\n## Version 1.30.0 → 1.31.0\n\n## Overview\n\nThis guide documents the changes to the Envoy External Processing HTTP filter between v1.30.0 (April 2024) and v1.31.0 (July 2024). The ext_proc filter enables external gRPC services to process HTTP requests and responses in flexible ways.\n\n**Summary of Major Changes:**\n- New `observability_mode` feature for monitoring HTTP traffic without blocking\n- Enhanced route cache control via new `route_cache_action` enum field\n- Support for deferred stream closure in observability mode\n- HTTP status code improvement for timeout errors\n- Deprecated `async_mode` in favor of `observability_mode`\n\n---\n\n## Breaking Changes\n\n### 1. HTTP Status Code for External Processor Timeouts\n\n**Impact:** Applications expecting `500 Internal Server Error` for ext_proc timeouts will now receive `504 Gateway Timeout`.\n\n**Details:**\n- **v1.30.0:** Timeout errors in external processor returned `500 Internal Server Error`\n- **v1.31.0:** Timeout errors now return `504 Gateway Timeout`\n- This is semantically more correct as it indicates the upstream service (external processor) is not responding\n\n**Migration Action:**\n- Update monitoring/alerting rules that depend on HTTP status codes for ext_proc failures\n- Adjust client-side retry logic if it differentiates between 5xx error codes\n- No configuration changes required\n\n**Source Files:**\n- `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.cc` - Filter implementation\n\n---\n\n## Deprecated Features\n\n### 1. `disable_clear_route_cache` Field (Field 11)\n\n**Status:** Deprecated but still functional with migration support\n\n**Details:**\n- **v1.30.0:** Boolean field that prevents route cache from being cleared\n- **v1.31.0:** Marked for deprecation via UDPA field migration annotation\n- **Recommended Replacement:** Use `route_cache_action` field instead\n\n**Migration Path:**\n```protobuf\n// v1.30.0 style (deprecated in v1.31.0)\ndisable_clear_route_cache: true\n\n// v1.31.0 style (recommended)\nroute_cache_action: RETAIN\n```\n\n**Behavior Mapping:**\n- `disable_clear_route_cache: true` → `route_cache_action: RETAIN`\n- `disable_clear_route_cache: false` (or unset) → `route_cache_action: DEFAULT`\n\n**Migration Timeline:**\n- v1.31.0: Both fields accepted, migration annotation present\n- Future versions: `disable_clear_route_cache` may be removed\n\n**YAML Configuration Example:**\n\nBefore:\n```yaml\nname: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\ntyped_config:\n  \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: ext_proc_service\n  disable_clear_route_cache: true\n```\n\nAfter:\n```yaml\nname: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\ntyped_config:\n  \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: ext_proc_service\n  route_cache_action: RETAIN\n```\n\n**Source Files:**\n- `api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/ext_proc.proto` (lines 250-251)\n- `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.cc` - Initialization logic\n- `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.h` - Field declaration\n\n### 2. `async_mode` (Field 4, marked as reserved in ExtProcOverrides)\n\n**Status:** Not implemented, marked as hidden\n\n**Details:**\n- Remains marked as `[#not-implemented-hide:]` in the ExtProcOverrides message\n- The new `observability_mode` at the filter configuration level provides similar functionality\n- Note: `async_mode` was never actually implemented in the filter\n\n**Migration Action:**\n- If you attempted to use `async_mode` in ExtProcOverrides, it will continue to be ignored\n- To enable asynchronous-like behavior, use `observability_mode` at the filter config level (see New Features section below)\n\n---\n\n## New Features\n\n### 1. Observability Mode\n\n**Availability:** New in v1.31.0\n\n**Purpose:** Enables \"Send and Go\" mode for external processors that only observe/monitor traffic without modifying it.\n\n**Configuration Field:**\n```protobuf\n// Field 17 in ExternalProcessor message\nbool observability_mode = 17;\n```\n\n**Key Characteristics:**\n- External processor receives HTTP request and response data without sending back responses\n- Messages are sent without pausing on filter chain iteration\n- Only `STREAMED` body processing mode is supported (other body modes are ignored)\n- `NONE` body mode (skip body) continues to work as expected\n- External processor may still close the stream to signal completion\n- Flow control is being developed but not yet complete\n\n**YAML Configuration Example:**\n```yaml\nname: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\ntyped_config:\n  \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: ext_proc_observability_service\n  processing_mode:\n    request_header_mode: SEND\n    response_header_mode: SEND\n    request_body_mode: STREAMED\n    response_body_mode: STREAMED\n  observability_mode: true\n  deferred_close_timeout:\n    seconds: 5\n```\n\n**Supported Processing Modes with observability_mode:**\n| Mode | Result | Notes |\n|------|--------|-------|\n| request_header_mode: SEND | ✓ Sent | Headers always sent |\n| response_header_mode: SEND | ✓ Sent | Headers always sent |\n| request_body_mode: STREAMED | ✓ Sent | Body streamed without blocking |\n| request_body_mode: BUFFERED | ⚠️ Ignored | Falls back to streaming behavior |\n| request_body_mode: BUFFERED_PARTIAL | ⚠️ Ignored | Falls back to streaming behavior |\n| request_body_mode: NONE | ✓ Skipped | Body not sent |\n| request_trailer_mode: SEND | ✓ Sent | Trailers sent if present |\n\n**Message Format:**\n- Requests include `observability_mode: true` flag in the ProcessingRequest\n- ProcessingResponse is ignored/not expected from the processor\n- Timeouts (message_timeout) do not apply in observability mode\n\n**Practical Use Cases:**\n- Monitoring/logging services that observe request/response headers and bodies\n- Distributed tracing integration\n- Audit logging systems\n- Traffic analytics services\n- Network diagnostic tools\n\n**Implementation Details:**\n- Uses `DeferredDeletableStream` wrapper for managing stream lifecycle\n- `ThreadLocalStreamManager` handles deferred stream closure\n- Streams may be held open longer than regular client-to-backend streams\n- `deferred_close_timeout` controls maximum stream lifetime\n\n**Source Files:**\n- `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.h` (lines 212, 275)\n- `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.cc` - observability mode handling\n\n### 2. Route Cache Action Enum\n\n**Availability:** New in v1.31.0\n\n**Purpose:** Provides explicit control over when the route cache should be cleared based on external processor responses.\n\n**Configuration Field:**\n```protobuf\n// Field 18 in ExternalProcessor message\nenum RouteCacheAction {\n  // The default behavior (consistent with v1.30.0)\n  DEFAULT = 0;\n\n  // Always clear the route cache\n  CLEAR = 1;\n\n  // Never clear the route cache (replaces disable_clear_route_cache)\n  RETAIN = 2;\n}\n\nRouteCacheAction route_cache_action = 18;\n```\n\n**Behavior Details:**\n\n#### DEFAULT Mode (Recommended for most users)\n- Route cache is cleared **only if** the external processor sets `clear_route_cache: true` in the response\n- Maintains backward compatibility with v1.30.0 behavior\n- Most flexible approach allowing per-request control\n\n```yaml\nroute_cache_action: DEFAULT\n```\n\n#### CLEAR Mode\n- Route cache is **always cleared** when external processor responds to request headers\n- Ignores the `clear_route_cache` field in processor response\n- Use when header modifications always require route recomputation\n\n```yaml\nroute_cache_action: CLEAR\n```\n\n#### RETAIN Mode\n- Route cache is **never cleared** regardless of processor response\n- Ignores the `clear_route_cache` field in processor response\n- Use when you know header modifications won't affect routing\n\n```yaml\nroute_cache_action: RETAIN\n```\n\n**When Route Cache Matters:**\nThe route cache affects whether modified headers trigger route recomputation:\n- Headers like `:authority`, `:scheme`, `:method`, and user-defined routing headers may affect route selection\n- Route modifications from external processor may be ignored if cache is not cleared\n- Example: If external processor changes `:authority` header, route cache must be cleared for new route to take effect\n\n**Interaction with Upstream Filters:**\n- Route cache clearing is ignored when ext_proc filter is in upstream filter chain\n- Statistics are tracked: `clear_route_cache_upstream_ignored`\n\n**YAML Configuration Examples:**\n\n```yaml\n# Example 1: Default behavior (recommended)\nname: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\ntyped_config:\n  \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: ext_proc_service\n  route_cache_action: DEFAULT\n\n# Example 2: Always clear route cache\nname: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\ntyped_config:\n  \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: ext_proc_service\n  route_cache_action: CLEAR\n\n# Example 3: Never clear route cache\nname: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\ntyped_config:\n  \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: ext_proc_service\n  route_cache_action: RETAIN\n```\n\n**Constraints:**\n- `disable_clear_route_cache` and `route_cache_action` are mutually exclusive\n- Attempting to set both will result in an error: \"disable_clear_route_cache and route_cache_action can not be set at the same time\"\n- If `disable_clear_route_cache: true` is set, it is automatically converted to `route_cache_action: RETAIN`\n\n**Source Files:**\n- `api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/ext_proc.proto` (lines 105-120, 253-258)\n- `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.cc` - Route cache action handling\n- `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/processor_state.cc` - Route cache clearing logic\n\n### 3. Deferred Close Timeout\n\n**Availability:** New in v1.31.0\n\n**Purpose:** Controls the maximum duration a gRPC stream to the external processor may remain open in observability mode.\n\n**Configuration Field:**\n```protobuf\n// Field 19 in ExternalProcessor message\ngoogle.protobuf.Duration deferred_close_timeout = 19;\n```\n\n**Default Value:**\n- `5000` milliseconds (5 seconds) if not specified\n\n**Why It's Needed:**\nIn observability mode, streams may be held open longer than the client-to-backend stream lifetime. This timeout prevents indefinite stream lifetime.\n\n**When It Applies:**\n- Only used in `observability_mode: true` configurations\n- Ignored in standard synchronous mode\n\n**YAML Configuration Example:**\n```yaml\nname: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\ntyped_config:\n  \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: ext_proc_service\n  observability_mode: true\n  deferred_close_timeout:\n    seconds: 10\n    # Optional: nanos: 0\n\n# Alternative: 2.5 seconds\ndeferred_close_timeout:\n  seconds: 2\n  nanos: 500000000\n\n# Alternative: 100 milliseconds\ndeferred_close_timeout:\n  nanos: 100000000\n```\n\n**Validation Rules:**\n- Maximum allowed: 3600 seconds (1 hour)\n- Minimum allowed: 0 (immediate timeout, useful for testing)\n- Values follow protobuf Duration format validation\n\n**Implementation Details:**\n- Uses `DeferredDeletableStream` struct to wrap streams with timeout\n- `ThreadLocalStreamManager` manages deferred closure with timers\n- Timer name: `derferred_close_timer` (note: contains typo in source code)\n\n**Source Files:**\n- `api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/ext_proc.proto` (lines 260-265)\n- `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.h` (lines 150-171, 214, 278)\n- `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.cc` - Deferred close handling\n\n---\n\n## Migration Steps\n\n### Step 1: Audit Current Configuration (v1.30.0)\n\nIdentify all ext_proc filter configurations in your Envoy setup:\n\n```bash\n# Find all ext_proc filter configurations\ngrep -r \"envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\" /path/to/configs/\ngrep -r \"ext_proc\" /path/to/configs/\n```\n\nDocument:\n- All `disable_clear_route_cache` settings\n- All `async_mode` references (should be none if not implemented)\n- Whether `observability_mode`-like behavior is needed\n\n### Step 2: Plan Field Migrations\n\n#### For `disable_clear_route_cache` Users:\n\n**Option A: Migrate to `route_cache_action`** (Recommended)\n```yaml\n# Old (v1.30.0)\ndisable_clear_route_cache: false\n\n# New (v1.31.0)\nroute_cache_action: DEFAULT\n```\n\n```yaml\n# Old (v1.30.0)\ndisable_clear_route_cache: true\n\n# New (v1.31.0)\nroute_cache_action: RETAIN\n```\n\n**Option B: No Action Required**\n- Both fields will be supported in v1.31.0\n- Migration can be deferred to a future version\n- Automatic conversion happens: `disable_clear_route_cache: true` → `route_cache_action: RETAIN`\n\n#### For `async_mode` Users:\n- If used in ExtProcOverrides, the field will continue to be ignored\n- No migration path exists yet (async_mode was never implemented)\n- For monitoring use cases, consider `observability_mode` instead\n\n### Step 3: Enable New Features (Optional)\n\nIf you need observability/monitoring capabilities:\n\n```yaml\nname: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\ntyped_config:\n  \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: ext_proc_monitoring_service\n  processing_mode:\n    request_header_mode: SEND\n    response_header_mode: SEND\n    request_body_mode: STREAMED\n    response_body_mode: STREAMED\n  observability_mode: true\n  deferred_close_timeout:\n    seconds: 5\n```\n\n### Step 4: Update External Processor Service\n\n**If Using Standard Synchronous Mode:**\n- No changes required to external processor service\n- Continue implementing `ProcessingRequest` → `ProcessingResponse` handlers\n\n**If Using Observability Mode:**\n- Update external processor to handle `observability_mode: true` flag in requests\n- Process and log/monitor data from requests\n- Do NOT send back `ProcessingResponse` messages (they will be ignored)\n- May close stream early with `grpc.stream.close()`\n\n### Step 5: Test Configuration\n\n**Validation Steps:**\n1. Validate configuration syntax (proto validation)\n2. Test with new Envoy v1.31.0 binary\n3. Verify external processor connectivity and behavior\n4. Test header modifications with new route cache action setting\n5. Monitor HTTP status codes for timeout errors (now 504 instead of 500)\n\n**Test Case Examples:**\n\n```yaml\n# Test 1: Route cache action behavior\n---\nname: Test DEFAULT route cache action\nhttp_filters:\n  - name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n    typed_config:\n      \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n      grpc_service:\n        envoy_grpc:\n          cluster_name: ext_proc\n      route_cache_action: DEFAULT\n      processing_mode:\n        request_header_mode: SEND\n\n# External processor modifies :authority header\n# Route cache should clear ONLY if response has clear_route_cache: true\n\n---\nname: Test CLEAR route cache action\nhttp_filters:\n  - name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n    typed_config:\n      \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n      grpc_service:\n        envoy_grpc:\n          cluster_name: ext_proc\n      route_cache_action: CLEAR\n      processing_mode:\n        request_header_mode: SEND\n\n# External processor modifies :authority header\n# Route cache should ALWAYS clear, regardless of response\n\n---\nname: Test RETAIN route cache action\nhttp_filters:\n  - name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n    typed_config:\n      \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n      grpc_service:\n        envoy_grpc:\n          cluster_name: ext_proc\n      route_cache_action: RETAIN\n      processing_mode:\n        request_header_mode: SEND\n\n# External processor modifies headers\n# Route cache should NEVER clear\n\n---\nname: Test observability mode\nhttp_filters:\n  - name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n    typed_config:\n      \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n      grpc_service:\n        envoy_grpc:\n          cluster_name: ext_proc_monitoring\n      processing_mode:\n        request_body_mode: STREAMED\n        response_body_mode: STREAMED\n      observability_mode: true\n\n# Processor receives requests but doesn't send responses\n# Verify: stream closure after deferred_close_timeout\n```\n\n### Step 6: Monitor and Validate\n\n**Metrics to Monitor:**\n\n```\n# Route cache action metrics (new in v1.31.0)\nenvoy_http_ext_proc_clear_route_cache_ignored{...}\nenvoy_http_ext_proc_clear_route_cache_disabled{...}\nenvoy_http_ext_proc_clear_route_cache_upstream_ignored{...}\n\n# Existing metrics still available\nenvoy_http_ext_proc_streams_started{...}\nenvoy_http_ext_proc_stream_msgs_sent{...}\nenvoy_http_ext_proc_stream_msgs_received{...}\nenvoy_http_ext_proc_streams_failed{...}\nenvoy_http_ext_proc_message_timeouts{...}\n\n# Status code changes\nenvoy_http_<stat_prefix>_response_code_504{...}  # New in v1.31.0 (previously 500)\n```\n\n---\n\n## Behavioral Changes Summary\n\n### Status Code Changes\n\n| Scenario | v1.30.0 | v1.31.0 | Impact |\n|----------|---------|---------|--------|\n| External processor timeout | 500 | 504 | Upstream service unavailable |\n| gRPC stream error | 500 | 500 | Stream connection failure |\n| Failure mode allow | Pass-through | Pass-through | No change |\n\n**Implications:**\n- Client-side retry logic may need updates\n- Load balancer health checks may treat 504 differently\n- Monitoring/alerting rules should be reviewed\n\n### gRPC Tracing Context Headers\n\n**v1.31.0 Enhancement:**\n- `AsyncStreamImpl` and `GoogleAsyncStreamImpl` now propagate tracing context headers in bidirectional streams\n- Applies when using Envoy gRPC client or Google C++ gRPC client\n- Previously, tracing context was not being set for external services like ext_proc\n- This improves distributed tracing across ext_proc services\n\n---\n\n## Configuration Field Reference\n\n### Complete v1.31.0 ExternalProcessor Message\n\n```protobuf\nmessage ExternalProcessor {\n  // [1] Required: gRPC service configuration\n  config.core.v3.GrpcService grpc_service = 1;\n\n  // [2] Default: false - Allow processing to continue on gRPC errors\n  bool failure_mode_allow = 2;\n\n  // [3] Default: SEND for headers, NONE for bodies - Processing modes\n  ProcessingMode processing_mode = 3;\n\n  // [5] Default: [] - Request attributes to send to processor\n  repeated string request_attributes = 5;\n\n  // [6] Default: [] - Response attributes to send to processor\n  repeated string response_attributes = 6;\n\n  // [7] Default: 200ms - Timeout for processor messages\n  google.protobuf.Duration message_timeout = 7;\n\n  // [8] Default: \"\" - Additional stats prefix\n  string stat_prefix = 8;\n\n  // [9] Default: allow all except protected headers - Header mutation rules\n  config.common.mutation_rules.v3.HeaderMutationRules mutation_rules = 9;\n\n  // [10] Default: 0 (disabled) - Max override message timeout\n  google.protobuf.Duration max_message_timeout = 10;\n\n  // [11] DEPRECATED: Use route_cache_action instead\n  // Default: false - Don't clear route cache when processor requests\n  bool disable_clear_route_cache = 11;\n\n  // [12] Default: forward all - Header forwarding rules\n  HeaderForwardingRules forward_rules = 12;\n\n  // [13] Default: {} - Additional metadata for logging\n  google.protobuf.Struct filter_metadata = 13;\n\n  // [14] Default: false - Allow processor to override processing mode\n  bool allow_mode_override = 14;\n\n  // [15] Default: false - Ignore immediate_response from processor\n  bool disable_immediate_response = 15;\n\n  // [16] Default: [] - Dynamic metadata options\n  MetadataOptions metadata_options = 16;\n\n  // [17] Default: false - NEW: Observability/monitoring mode (Send and Go)\n  bool observability_mode = 17;\n\n  // [18] NEW: Route cache action (replaces disable_clear_route_cache)\n  // Default: DEFAULT\n  RouteCacheAction route_cache_action = 18;\n\n  // [19] NEW: Stream deferred close timeout in observability mode\n  // Default: 5000ms\n  google.protobuf.Duration deferred_close_timeout = 19;\n}\n\nenum RouteCacheAction {\n  DEFAULT = 0;  // Clear only if processor requests\n  CLEAR = 1;    // Always clear\n  RETAIN = 2;   // Never clear\n}\n\nmessage HeaderForwardingRules {\n  type.matcher.v3.ListStringMatcher allowed_headers = 1;\n  type.matcher.v3.ListStringMatcher disallowed_headers = 2;\n}\n\nmessage MetadataOptions {\n  message MetadataNamespaces {\n    repeated string untyped = 1;\n    repeated string typed = 2;\n  }\n  MetadataNamespaces forwarding_namespaces = 1;\n  MetadataNamespaces receiving_namespaces = 2;\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Testing Recommendations\n\n### Unit Test Strategy\n\n1. **Route Cache Action Tests**\n   - Verify DEFAULT mode respects `clear_route_cache` in response\n   - Verify CLEAR mode always clears regardless of response\n   - Verify RETAIN mode never clears regardless of response\n   - Test with upstream filter chain (should ignore all modes)\n\n2. **Observability Mode Tests**\n   - Verify `observability_mode: true` sends messages without waiting for responses\n   - Verify only STREAMED body mode is actually used\n   - Verify BUFFERED/BUFFERED_PARTIAL fall back to streaming\n   - Verify NONE mode skips body processing\n   - Verify stream closure after `deferred_close_timeout`\n\n3. **Status Code Tests**\n   - Verify timeout errors return 504 instead of 500\n   - Verify other errors still return appropriate codes\n   - Verify failure_mode_allow still works\n\n4. **Backward Compatibility Tests**\n   - Verify old configs with `disable_clear_route_cache` still work\n   - Verify automatic conversion to RETAIN works\n   - Verify both fields can't be set simultaneously\n\n### Integration Test Strategy\n\n1. **External Processor Integration**\n   - Test with real external processor service\n   - Verify request/response format unchanged\n   - Verify header modifications work as before\n   - Test with observability_mode processor\n\n2. **Header Modification Tests**\n   - Modify :authority header and verify route recalculation\n   - Modify custom routing headers\n   - Verify route cache clearing behavior with each action mode\n\n3. **Performance Tests**\n   - Measure impact of observability_mode on throughput\n   - Compare stream closure behavior with deferred_close_timeout\n\n4. **Upgrade Tests**\n   - Run existing v1.30.0 configs on v1.31.0 binary\n   - Verify graceful behavior with new fields unset\n   - Test both field migration approaches\n\n---\n\n## Rollback Guidance\n\n### If Issues Occur\n\n**Option 1: Immediate Rollback**\n1. Revert to Envoy v1.30.0 binary\n2. No configuration changes needed (v1.30.0 ignores v1.31.0-only fields)\n3. Verify service stabilization\n\n**Option 2: Downgrade with Configuration Update**\nIf you updated configs to use v1.31.0 features:\n\n```yaml\n# Before rollback (v1.31.0 config)\nroute_cache_action: CLEAR\nobservability_mode: true\n\n# Rollback (v1.30.0 compatible)\ndisable_clear_route_cache: false  # Equivalent to DEFAULT\n# Remove observability_mode (not supported)\n# Remove deferred_close_timeout (not supported)\n```\n\n### Common Issues and Resolution\n\n**Issue: \"disable_clear_route_cache and route_cache_action can not be set at the same time\"**\n- **Cause:** Both fields set in configuration\n- **Fix:** Use only `route_cache_action`, remove `disable_clear_route_cache`\n- **Workaround:** Temporarily revert to v1.30.0\n\n**Issue: Observability mode processor not receiving messages**\n- **Cause:** Messages might be sent before stream is fully established\n- **Fix:** Add delay in processor startup or ensure it's listening before Envoy sends\n- **Fix:** Check that `processing_mode` is configured correctly\n\n**Issue: Stream timeouts in observability mode**\n- **Cause:** `deferred_close_timeout` too short for processor\n- **Fix:** Increase `deferred_close_timeout` value\n- **Example:** Increase from default 5s to 10s or more\n\n**Issue: Route cache not clearing as expected**\n- **Cause:** Wrong `route_cache_action` mode selected\n- **Debug:** Enable debug logging: `--log-level debug`\n- **Debug:** Check statistics: `clear_route_cache_ignored`, `clear_route_cache_disabled`\n\n---\n\n## Proto File Changes\n\n### Files Modified in v1.31.0\n\n#### `api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/ext_proc.proto`\n\n**Key Changes:**\n- Added import: `udpa/annotations/migrate.proto`\n- Updated `[#next-free-field]` comment: 18 → 20\n- Added `RouteCacheAction` enum (lines 105-120)\n- Added field migration annotation to `disable_clear_route_cache` (line 251)\n- Added `route_cache_action` field (field 18, lines 253-258)\n- Added `deferred_close_timeout` field (field 19, lines 260-265)\n\n**Line-by-Line Changes:**\n```protobuf\n// Line 14: NEW IMPORT\nimport \"udpa/annotations/migrate.proto\";\n\n// Line 101: UPDATED Header mutation | ✓ | ✓ Unchanged | No action needed |\n| Streaming bodies | ✓ | ✓ Unchanged | No action needed |\n| Dynamic metadata | ✓ | ✓ Unchanged | No action needed |\n\n---\n\n## Best Practices for v1.31.0\n\n### 1. **Route Cache Management**\n- Use `route_cache_action: DEFAULT` for most cases (allows per-request control)\n- Use `route_cache_action: CLEAR` only if all processor responses require route recalculation\n- Use `route_cache_action: RETAIN` only if processor never modifies routing-relevant headers\n\n### 2. **Observability Mode**\n- Only enable for monitoring/logging processors\n- Don't enable if processor needs to modify requests/responses\n- Ensure processor implementation handles one-way messaging\n- Set appropriate `deferred_close_timeout` for your use case (5-10 seconds typical)\n\n### 3. **Processing Mode with Observability**\n- Limit to essential fields (headers, bodies needed for logging)\n- Avoid `BUFFERED` modes as they're converted to `STREAMED` anyway\n- Consider bandwidth impact of streaming large bodies\n\n### 4. **Monitoring and Alerting**\n- Update status code alerts (504 for timeouts, not 500)\n- Add metrics tracking for route cache actions\n- Monitor `deferred_close_timeout` for observability streams\n\n### 5. **Documentation**\n- Document which route cache action mode each processor requires\n- Maintain runbooks for migration issues\n- Track external processor compatibility with v1.31.0\n\n---\n\n## Additional Resources\n\n### Envoy Documentation\n- [ext_proc Filter Configuration
